Command Engineer2.write_new_code executed: The file /home/mas-metagpt/Desktop/MetaGPT/workspace/fruit_distribution.py has been successfully created, with content:
def fruit_distribution(s, n):
    """
    In this task, you will be given a string that represents a number of apples and oranges 
    that are distributed in a basket of fruit. This basket contains 
    apples, oranges, and mango fruits. Given the string that represents the total number of 
    the oranges and apples and an integer that represents the total number of the fruits 
    in the basket, return the number of mango fruits in the basket.
    
    For example:
    fruit_distribution("5 apples and 6 oranges", 19) -> 19 - 5 - 6 = 8
    fruit_distribution("0 apples and 1 oranges", 3) -> 3 - 0 - 1 = 2
    fruit_distribution("2 apples and 3 oranges", 100) -> 100 - 2 - 3 = 95
    fruit_distribution("100 apples and 1 oranges", 120) -> 120 - 100 - 1 = 19
    """
    # Extract the number of apples and oranges from the string
    parts = s.split()
    apples = int(parts[0])  # First part is the number of apples
    oranges = int(parts[2])  # Third part is the number of oranges
    
    # Calculate the number of mangoes
    mangoes = n - apples - oranges
    
    return mangoes

import unittest
from fruit_distribution import fruit_distribution

class TestFruitDistribution(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_fruit_distribution(self):
        # Test cases to validate the fruit_distribution function
        self.assertEqual(fruit_distribution("5 apples and 6 oranges", 19), 8)
        self.assertEqual(fruit_distribution("0 apples and 1 oranges", 3), 2)
        self.assertEqual(fruit_distribution("2 apples and 3 oranges", 100), 95)
        self.assertEqual(fruit_distribution("100 apples and 1 oranges", 120), 19)
        self.assertEqual(fruit_distribution("10 apples and 10 oranges", 50), 30)
        self.assertEqual(fruit_distribution("1 apples and 0 oranges", 1), 0)
        self.assertEqual(fruit_distribution("0 apples and 0 oranges", 0), 0)
        self.assertEqual(fruit_distribution("3 apples and 4 oranges", 10), 3)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    unittest.main()

001|def fruit_distribution(s, n):
002|    """
003|    In this task, you will be given a string that represents a number of apples and oranges 
004|    that are distributed in a basket of fruit. This basket contains 
005|    apples, oranges, and mango fruits. Given the string that represents the total number of 
006|    the oranges and apples and an integer that represents the total number of the fruits 
007|    in the basket, return the number of mango fruits in the basket.
008|    
009|    For example:
010|    fruit_distribution("5 apples and 6 oranges", 19) -> 19 - 5 - 6 = 8
011|    fruit_distribution("0 apples and 1 oranges", 3) -> 3 - 0 - 1 = 2
012|    fruit_distribution("2 apples and 3 oranges", 100) -> 100 - 2 - 3 = 95
013|    fruit_distribution("100 apples and 1 oranges", 120) -> 120 - 100 - 1 = 19
014|    """
015|    # Extract the number of apples and oranges from the string
016|    parts = s.split()
017|    apples = int(parts[0])  # First part is the number of apples
018|    oranges = int(parts[2])  # Third part is the number of oranges
019|    
020|    # Calculate the number of mangoes
021|    mangoes = n - apples - oranges
022|    
023|    return mangoes

Command Engineer2.write_new_code executed: The file /home/mas-metagpt/Desktop/MetaGPT/workspace/fruit_distribution.py has been successfully created, with content:
import re

def fruit_distribution(s, n):
    """
    In this task, you will be given a string that represents a number of apples and oranges 
    that are distributed in a basket of fruit. This basket contains 
    apples, oranges, and mango fruits. Given the string that represents the total number of 
    the oranges and apples and an integer that represents the total number of the fruits 
    in the basket, return the number of mango fruits in the basket.
    
    For example:
    fruit_distribution("5 apples and 6 oranges", 19) -> 19 - 5 - 6 = 8
    fruit_distribution("0 apples and 1 oranges", 3) -> 3 - 0 - 1 = 2
    fruit_distribution("2 apples and 3 oranges", 100) -> 100 - 2 - 3 = 95
    fruit_distribution("100 apples and 1 oranges", 120) -> 120 - 100 - 1 = 19
    """
    # Extract the number of apples and oranges from the string using regular expressions
    apples = int(re.search(r'(\d+) apples', s).group(1))
    oranges = int(re.search(r'(\d+) oranges', s).group(1))
    
    # Calculate the number of mangoes
    mangoes = n - apples - oranges
    
    return mangoes
